\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{float\_equals()}{float\_equals()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Epsilon\+Type  = float, typename LNumber , typename RNumber $>$ \\
bool xlnt\+::detail\+::float\+\_\+equals (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const LNumber \&}]{lhs,  }\item[{const RNumber \&}]{rhs,  }\item[{int}]{epsilon\+\_\+scale = {\ttfamily 20} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Floating point equality requires a bit of fuzzing due to the imprecise nature of fp calculation References\+: 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Several blogs/articles were referenced with the following being the most useful -- \href{https://randomascii.wordpress.com/2012/02/25/comparing-floating-point-numbers-2012-edition/}{\texttt{ https\+://randomascii.\+wordpress.\+com/2012/02/25/comparing-\/floating-\/point-\/numbers-\/2012-\/edition/}} -- \href{http://realtimecollisiondetection.net/blog/?p=89}{\texttt{ http\+://realtimecollisiondetection.\+net/blog/?p=89}}
\item Testing Frameworks \{Catch2, Boost, Google\}, primarily for selecting the default scale factor -- None of these even remotely agree
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacexlnt_1_1detail_a275073ae83b76e22d85555c973553504}\label{namespacexlnt_1_1detail_a275073ae83b76e22d85555c973553504}}
